26 EXCURSIE EXCURSION <p class="MsoPlainText" style="margin-top: 6pt;"><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">Dear colleagues,</font></p> 
  <p class="MsoPlainText" style="margin-top: 6pt;"><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">On Saturday, November 24<sup>th</sup>, we will organize a field trip in a woodland area in Ghimpați, Giurgiu County.&nbsp;</font></p> 
  <p class="MsoPlainText" style="margin-top: 6pt;"><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">In the morning we will visit the Ghimpați Pheasantry (located in Ghimpați Forest), one of the oldest in Romania with a tradition of over 90 years. After this visit, we will be transported to the Albele Forest and we will walk some 4 km through the forest during which we will have the chance to observe and admire the autumn nature. We will reach the Albele Chalet where a traditional lunch will be served. The main attraction will be whole lamb roasted on a spit and tender lamb chops with a side dish of seasoned baked potatoes. All served dishes will be accompanied by local wines and spirits (țuică).</font></p> 
  <p class="MsoPlainText" style="margin-top: 6pt;"><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">In the afternoon, we will go to special forestry observatories in the woods, where hopefully we will have the opportunity to watch some wildlife (most likely wild boar and roe deer).</font></p> 
  <p class="MsoPlainText" style="margin-top: 6pt;"><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">We advise you to bring outdoor gear (boots, winter coat / rain coat, warm trousers and sweater, etc.) as the November weather in Romania can get cold and rainy, especially in wooded areas.</font></p> 
  <p class="MsoPlainText" style="margin-top: 6pt;"><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">The fee for the field trip is 20 EURO or 90 RON/person. Transport, refreshments, and lunch are included.</font></p> 
  <div><br /></div> <p> </p> 
  <p><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
  <o:AllowPNG/>
 </o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
</xml><![endif]--><font size="2" face="verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif"></font></p> 
  <p> </p> 
  <p><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">Dear colleagues,</font></p> 
  <p><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">On Saturday, November 24<sup>th</sup>, we will organize a field trip in a woodland area in Ghimpați, Giurgiu County.&nbsp;</font></p> 
  <p><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">In the morning we will visit the Ghimpați Pheasantry (located in Ghimpați Forest), one of the oldest in Romania with a tradition of over 90 years. After this visit, we will be transported to the Albele Forest and we will walk some 4 km through the forest during which we will have the chance to observe and admire the autumn nature. We will reach the Albele Chalet where a traditional lunch will be served. The main attraction will be whole lamb roasted on a spit and tender lamb chops with a side dish of seasoned baked potatoes. All served dishes will be accompanied by local wines and spirits (țuică).</font></p> 
  <p><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">In the afternoon, we will go to special forestry observatories in the woods, where hopefully we will have the opportunity to watch some wildlife (most likely wild boar and roe deer).</font></p> 
  <p><font size="4" face="times new roman, times, serif">We advise you to bring outdoor gear (boots, winter coat / rain coat, warm trousers and sweater, etc.) as the November weather in Romania can get cold and rainy, especially in wooded areas.</font></p>

4 Text header Text header <div align="center"><strong><font size="6" face="verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif">International Zoological <br />Congress of <br />“Grigore Antipa” Museum</font><font size="6" face="verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif"> </font></strong> </div> <div align="center"><font face="verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif"><strong><font size="6">International Zoological <br />Congress</font></strong></font><font face="verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif"><strong><font size="6"> of <br />“Grigore Antipa” Museum</font></strong></font></div>
  <div align="center"> </div> N 1
14 Dragi colegi, Dear colleagues, <div align="justify">MUZEUL NAŢIONAL DE ISTORIE NATURALĂ „GRIGORE ANTIPA”, în parteneriat cu ACADEMIA ROMÂNĂ – Secția de Științe Biologice și UNIVERSITATEA DIN BUCUREȘTI – Facultatea de Biologie, Departamentul de Biochimie și Biologie Moleculară, are deosebita plăcere de a vă invita să participaţi la <em>Al 10-lea Congres Internațional de Zoologie al Muzeului „Grigore Antipa”</em> (CZGA 2018) care se va desfăşura în perioada 21-24 noiembrie 2018, <!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
  <o:TargetScreenSize>800x600</o:TargetScreenSize>
 </o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
</xml><![endif]-->în amfiteatrul “Ion Heliade Rădulescu” al Academiei
Române (Calea Victoriei nr. 125, Bucureşti, România).</div> 
  <p align="justify"> </p> <div align="justify">“GRIGORE ANTIPA” NATIONAL MUSEUM OF NATURAL HISTORY, in partnership with THE ROMANIAN ACADEMY – Section of Biological Sciences and UNIVERSITY OF BUCHAREST – Faculty of Biology, Department of Biochemistry and Molecular Biology, gladly invites you to participate to <em>The 10<sup>th</sup> International Zoological Congress of “Grigore Antipa” Museum</em> (CZGA 2018), during 21-24 November 2018, <!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
  <o:TargetScreenSize>800x600</o:TargetScreenSize>
 </o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
</xml><![endif]-->in the “Ion Heliade Rădulescu” Amphitheatre of the
Romanian Academy (Calea Victoriei Blvd., no. 125, Bucharest, Romania).</div>

6 ARII TEMATICE SYMPOSIA <p align="justify"> <br />Congresul va fi consacrat prezentării de <strong>lucrări cu specific zoologic</strong> din următoarele arii tematice:
</p> 
  <p align="justify"> </p> 
  <p align="justify"> </p> 
  <p align="justify">1. <strong>Taxonomie. Faunistică. Zoogeografie</strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">2. <strong>Filogenie, Evoluție și Sistematică</strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">3. <strong>Paleontologie </strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">4. <strong>Ecologie </strong></p> 
  <p>5. <strong>Specii invazive </strong> </p>
  <p align="justify">6. <strong>Parazitismul în regnul animal </strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">7. <strong>Conservarea biodiversităţii </strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">8. <strong>Cercetarea şi valorificarea patrimoniului muzeal de ştiinţele naturii
  <br /><br /></strong> </p> <p align="justify"> <br />The Congress will be devoted to presenting <strong>zoological papers</strong> with the following thematic:
</p> 
  <p align="justify"> </p> 
  <p align="justify"> </p> 
  <p align="justify">1. <strong>Taxonomy. Faunistics. Zoogeography </strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">2. <strong>Phylogenetics, Evolution and Systematics </strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">3. <strong>Palaeontology</strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">4. <strong>Ecology</strong></p> 
  <p>5. <strong>Invasive species </strong> </p>
  <p align="justify">6. <strong>Parasitism in the animal kingdom </strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">7. <strong>Biodiversity conservation </strong> </p> 
  <p align="justify">8. <strong>Studies and recovery of the natural history museum patrimony</strong> <br /><br /> </p> Y 50
7 PROGRAM ŞTIINŢIFIC SCIENTIFIC PROGRAM <span style="color: #000000;"> 
    <p class="MsoNormal"> <span style="font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, serif;"> </span></p>
